This is our go to pho place. The restaurant is clean and food is good. Things we like: rare steak pho, steak over rice, chicken banh mi, egg rolls, charbroiled pork with vermicelli noodles.

Also, take out is always nicely packed. If we order pho, we'll reheat the soup at home, then pour the simmering soup over the noodles and steak in a large bowl. Don't cook the noodles as you heat the soup, or it will fall apart and turn to mush!< /Text>

The new pho place just opened recently. We came here twice (both dinner time) and liked it very much. The interior is newly remodeled and beautiful. The pho broth is sweet and cinnamon-y than other pho places but I like it. We have tried several other dishes and liked them too. The BBQ meat is a bit on the salty side for my taste, the chicken is white meat so it's on the dry side. The seasoning is good though.   Overall, I enjoy coming here. It's so close to Cowan height so we don't have to drive to other pho places. If you like pho, give it a try.</review>

<user>116774522915247595588<//user>< username>
Vinnie Nguyen</username>
<Date>1568246519230</Date><rate>5</rate>< text>
Finding a good Pho restaurant in Little Saigon? Easy
Finding a good Pho restaurant anywhere else in OC? Hard

This is probably the best Pho restaurant in Tustin, and if it was in Little Saigon, it would probably get a cult following as well. Decor is very hip and modern. Oversized wood chairs and floor give the space a warm feel and lots of natural light brighten up the place.

The broth is packed with aromatics. The cinnamon & star anise are very pronounced. I feel the brisket could be more tender. They bring your utensils out in this neat little woven basket.

Only down side I've seen here is the slow service, especially during the lunch rush. It took 15 minutes to get our food out to us. That's an eternity when you're talking Vietnamese restaurant terms.

Overall, solid spot for Pho and I believe I'll keep returning.</text>

<user_name>Karla Davalos</user_name><Time>1560459254912<//Time>< text>
The environment of the place is really nice and comforting, i arrived and got seated right away but they did take long to take my order i want to say it was atleast 10min before i had to stare at the waiter and then he came and took my order. I did like that he mentioned the lunch special which was basically what i was ordering so that was nice . The broth its self tasted really bland to me, im not one to add sriracha or the "brown sauce" to my pho and i did to this one and i added quite alot. I got the chicken pho and to me even though the broth itself was boiling hot the chikens texture just seemed thick and dull. The lunch special came with 2 eggrolls and they actually forgot to bring them out to me, i had to remind the waiter that my order also came with eggrolls. I was upset with the eggrolls because they weren't hot they were warm but ive had eggrolls where they are still cooking on the plate. The only reason im not giving it a 1 star is because the pho was hot and it stayed hot till the moment i finished it and it didnt look thick like most pho get when they start to cool down. Would i come back , no i wouldn't . Would i recommend it to people? no, but the place was pretty packed with people but this is my opinon.< /text>

None< /pictures>
<text>Rosie's is an okay bbq spot in the West Valley. The meats are actually pretty good, especially the chicken and tri tip, which they are known for. It is not a particularly great place atmosphere wise. It is rather dark inside and on the outside, painted a drab brownish color that makes it difficult to see if it's open..and it does not stand out from the street. The staff up front is mostly high school /college aged kids..they seem to come and go quite frequently, no doubt the pay isn't higher than minimum. Service is therefore not great..like ordering from a fast food joint. The owner is often around, but don't expect her to say anything /greet customers..she usually is secluded in a cubicle of sorts near the register, eating and reading. Honestly, if it weren't the fact that this about the only bbq place around, I'd stop coming by from time to time..it's too dark, and the service is non existent. Better to take food away.< /text><rating>3<//rating></record></dataset><record>

Kevin helped me buy my first home and I will definitely be recommending him to any of my friends who are looking to buy in the future.

I was referred to Kevin via a coworker, and was very happy with the referral. As a first time homebuyer, Kevin was able to answer all of my many, many questions that I had throughout the process of buying my house (seriously, I had a lot of questions).

When we looked at houses, I never felt like he was trying to "sell" me on any house in particular - for me this was so important, since as a big people-pleaser, I can sometimes convince myself that I like something, even if I don't, simply because someone is doing a good job selling me on it.

The house that I purchased was older and Kevin really helped to walk me through the repair request process after the inspection. He worked with me to review my list of repairs and edit it down to a list of must-have items to make sure both the seller and myself felt like we got what we needed to lift the inspection contingency. He did a great job negotiating with the seller so I didn't have to compromise on any of my must have items. After the repairs were complete, he called up each of the contractors to talk to them about the repairs that were done and get their feedback on the house, which is something I wouldn't have thought to do as a first time homebuyer, but something that I appreciated.

Buying my first home was by far, the biggest purchase I've ever made, which made it exciting, but quite stressful. Kevin helped to smooth out the process as well as make me feel comfortable and knowledgeable about the decision I was making, which I am very appreciative of.</Review>
